----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

CLS()

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

DIS := (((2 * NE) * FA) / (NE + FA))

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

NU := 0

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

DO

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

NU := (NU + 1)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

HY := (((MM ** 2) / (F(NU) * C)) / 1000)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

NEAR := ((HY * DIS) / (HY + (DIS - (F(NU) / 1000))))

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

FAR := ((HY * DIS) / (HY - (DIS - (F(NU) / 1000))))

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

CLS()

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

AT(9 2 )

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

PRINT("f")

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

PRINT(F(NU))

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

<nl>

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

FAR := (FA + 1)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

ENDIF

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

UNTIL (((NEAR < NE) AND (FAR > FA)) OR (NU = 38))

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

FRAN

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

C% := (INT((5 * ABS(RND() )) ) + 1)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

hamu

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

D%

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

B%

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

P% := 95

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

S% := 2800

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

H% := 3000

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

E := 200

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

Y% := 3

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

A% := 1000

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

I% := 5

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

Q% := 1

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

START::

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

D% := 0

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

START1::

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

B% := VIEW(1 (("HAMURABI: LAST YEAR " + GEN$(D% 4 )) + " STARVED,") )

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

B% := VIEW(1 (GEN$(I% 4 ) + " ARRIVED.") )

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

P% := (P% + I%)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

IF (Q% = 0)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

P% := INT((P% / 2) )

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

B% := VIEW(1 "**PLAGUE**" )

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

ENDIF

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

B% := VIEW(1 ("POPULATION IS " + GEN$(P% 4 )) )

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

B% := VIEW(1 (("THE CITY OWNS " + GEN$(A% 4 )) + " ACRES.") )

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

B% := VIEW(1 (("WE HARVESTED " + GEN$(Y% 4 )) + " BUSHELS PER ACRE.") )

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

C% := 1

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

B% := VIEW(1 (("RATS ATE " + GEN$(E 4 )) + " BUSHELS.") )

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

B% := VIEW(1 (("YOU NOW HAVE " + GEN$(S% 4 )) + " BUSHELS IN STORE.") )

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

FRAN

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

Y% := (C% + 17)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

B% := VIEW(1 (("HAMURABI: LAND IS TRADING AT " + GEN$(Y% 4 )) + " BUSHELS PER ACRE.") )

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

C% := 1

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

BUY::

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

B% := VIEW(1 "HOW MANY ACRES OF LAND DO YOU WISH TO BUY?" )

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

AT(1 2 )

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

PRINT(">")

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------



----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

Q%

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

IF (Q% < 0)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

GOTO GBYE

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

ELSEIF (Q% = 0)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

GOTO SELL

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

ENDIF

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

B% := ((Y% * Q%) - S%)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

IF (B% < 0)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

GOTO SOLD

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

ELSEIF (B% = 0)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

GOTO S1

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

ENDIF

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

BUSH

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

GOTO BUY

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

S2::

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

ACRES

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

GOTO BUY

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

S1::

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

A% := (A% + Q%)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

S% := (S% - (Y% * Q%))

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

C% := 0

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

GOTO NOGRAIN

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

SELL::

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

B% := VIEW(1 "TO SELL?" )

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

AT(1 2 )

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

PRINT(">")

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------



----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

Q%

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

IF (Q% < 0)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

GOTO GBYE

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

ELSEIF (Q% = 0)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

GOTO SOLD

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

ENDIF

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

Q% := (UMIN Q%)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

IF ((A% + Q%) < 0)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

GOTO S2

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

ENDIF

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

SOLD::

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

A% := (A% + Q%)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

S% := (S% - (Y% * Q%))

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

C% := 0

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

SOLD1::

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

TIMESIDE

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

D := WATCH

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

N := ((360 / 365.242191) * D)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

NU := (N / 360)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

NU := INTF(NU )

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

N := (N - (NU * 360))

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

M := ((N + 279.403303) - 282.768422)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

IF (M < 0)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

M := (M + 360)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

ENDIF

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

M := SIN(RAD(M ) )

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

EU := (((360 / PI()) * 0.016713) * M)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

GEO := ((N + EU) + 279.403303)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

IF (GEO > 360)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

GEO := (GEO - 360)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

ENDIF

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

GEL := 0

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

DEC := ((SIN(RAD(GEL ) ) * COS(RAD(23.441884 ) )) + ((COS(RAD(GEL ) ) * SIN(RAD(23.441884 ) )) * SIN(RAD(GEO ) )))

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

DEC := DEG(ASIN(DEC ) )

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

Y := ((SIN(RAD(GEO ) ) * COS(RAD(23.441884 ) )) - (TAN(RAD(GEL ) ) * SIN(RAD(23.441884 ) )))

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

X := COS(RAD(GEO ) )

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

AS := (Y / X)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

AS := DEG(ATAN(AS ) )

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

IF ((X >= 0) AND (Y >= 0))

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

WHILE ((AS < 0) OR (AS > 90))

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

IF (AS < 0)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

AS := (AS + 180)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

ELSEIF (AS > 0)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

AS := (AS - 180)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

ENDIF

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

ENDWH

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

ELSEIF ((Y >= 0) AND (X < 0))

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

WHILE ((AS < 90) OR (AS > 180))

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

IF (AS < 90)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

AS := (AS + 180)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

ELSEIF (AS > 180)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

AS := (AS - 180)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

ENDIF

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

ENDWH

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

ELSEIF ((Y < 0) AND (X < 0))

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

WHILE ((AS < 180) OR (AS > 270))

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

IF (AS < 180)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

AS := (AS + 180)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

ELSEIF (AS > 270)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

AS := (AS - 180)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

ENDIF

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

ENDWH

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

ELSEIF ((Y < 0) AND (X >= 0))

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

WHILE ((AS < 270) OR (AS > 360))

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

IF (AS < 270)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

AS := (AS + 180)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

ELSEIF (AS > 360)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

AS := (AS - 180)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

ENDIF

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

ENDWH

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

ENDIF

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

AS := (AS / 15)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

LST := (GST + (LNG / 15))

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

NU := INTF((LST / 24) )

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

LST := (LST - (24 * NU))

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

ALT := (LST - AS)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

NU := INTF((ALT / 24) )

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

AS := (ALT - (24 * NU))

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

AS := (AS * 15)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

CH := SIN(RAD(AS ) )

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

ALT := ((SIN(RAD(DEC ) ) * SIN(RAD(LAT ) )) + ((COS(RAD(DEC ) ) * COS(RAD(LAT ) )) * COS(RAD(AS ) )))

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

ALT := DEG(ASIN(ALT ) )

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

AZI := ((SIN(RAD(DEC ) ) - (SIN(RAD(LAT ) ) * SIN(RAD(ALT ) ))) / (COS(RAD(LAT ) ) * COS(RAD(ALT ) )))

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

AZI := DEG(ACOS(AZI ) )

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

IF (CH >= 0)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

AZI := (360 - AZI)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

ENDIF

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

CLS()

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

PRINT("   Sun's position")

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

NU

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

JD := (2415020.5 + DAYS(DY MO YR ))

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

S := (JD - 2451545)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

T := (S / 36525)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

T0 := ((6.697374588 + (2400.051336 * T)) + (0.000025862 * (T ** 2)))

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

NU := INTF((T0 / 24) )

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

T0 := (T0 - (24 * NU))

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

<nl>

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------



----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

DROP()

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

D := WATCH

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

N := ((360 / 365.242191) * D)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

NU := (N / 360)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

NU := INTF(NU )

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

N := (N - (NU * 360))

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

M := ((N + 279.403303) - 282.768422)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

IF (M < 0)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

M := (M + 360)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

ENDIF

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

M := SIN(RAD(M ) )

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

EU := (((360 / PI()) * 0.016713) * M)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

GEO := ((N + EU) + 279.403303)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

IF (GEO > 360)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

GEO := (GEO - 360)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

ENDIF

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

GEL := 0

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

DEC := ((SIN(RAD(GEL ) ) * COS(RAD(23.441884 ) )) + ((COS(RAD(GEL ) ) * SIN(RAD(23.441884 ) )) * SIN(RAD(GEO ) )))

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

DEC := DEG(ASIN(DEC ) )

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

Y := ((SIN(RAD(GEO ) ) * COS(RAD(23.441884 ) )) - (TAN(RAD(GEL ) ) * SIN(RAD(23.441884 ) )))

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

X := COS(RAD(GEO ) )

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

AS := (Y / X)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

AS := DEG(ATAN(AS ) )

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

IF ((X >= 0) AND (Y >= 0))

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

WHILE ((AS < 0) OR (AS > 90))

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

IF (AS < 0)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

AS := (AS + 180)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

ELSEIF (AS > 0)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

AS := (AS - 180)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

ENDIF

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

ENDWH

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

ELSEIF ((Y >= 0) AND (X < 0))

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

WHILE ((AS < 90) OR (AS > 180))

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

IF (AS < 90)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

AS := (AS + 180)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

ELSEIF (AS > 180)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

AS := (AS - 180)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

ENDIF

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

ENDWH

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

ELSEIF ((Y < 0) AND (X < 0))

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

WHILE ((AS < 180) OR (AS > 270))

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

IF (AS < 180)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

AS := (AS + 180)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

ELSEIF (AS > 270)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

AS := (AS - 180)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

ENDIF

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

ENDWH

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

ELSEIF ((Y < 0) AND (X >= 0))

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

WHILE ((AS < 270) OR (AS > 360))

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

IF (AS < 270)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

AS := (AS + 180)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

ELSEIF (AS > 360)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

AS := (AS - 180)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

ENDIF

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

ENDWH

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

ENDIF

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

AS := (AS / 15)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

LST := (GST + (LNG / 15))

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

NU := INTF((LST / 24) )

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

LST := (LST - (24 * NU))

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

ALT := (LST - AS)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

NU := INTF((ALT / 24) )

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

AS := (ALT - (24 * NU))

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

AS := (AS * 15)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

CH := SIN(RAD(AS ) )

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

ALT := ((SIN(RAD(DEC ) ) * SIN(RAD(LAT ) )) + ((COS(RAD(DEC ) ) * COS(RAD(LAT ) )) * COS(RAD(AS ) )))

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

ALT := DEG(ASIN(ALT ) )

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

AZI := ((SIN(RAD(DEC ) ) - (SIN(RAD(LAT ) ) * SIN(RAD(ALT ) ))) / (COS(RAD(LAT ) ) * COS(RAD(ALT ) )))

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

AZI := DEG(ACOS(AZI ) )

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

IF (CH >= 0)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

AZI := (360 - AZI)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

ENDIF

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

CLS()

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

PRINT("   Sun's position")

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

JD := (2415020.5 + DAYS(DY MO YR ))

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

S := (JD - 2451545)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

T := (S / 36525)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

T0 := ((6.697374588 + (2400.051336 * T)) + (0.000025862 * (T ** 2)))

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

NU := INTF((T0 / 24) )

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

T0 := (T0 - (24 * NU))

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

MON := MI

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

MON := (MON / 60)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

UT := (HR + MON)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

UT := (UT * 1.002737909)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

GST := (T0 + UT)

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

NU := INTF((GST / 24) )

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------

GST := (GST - (24 * NU))

----------------------------------------infix-----------------------------------
